The phenotypes were nine to three to three to one (9:3:3:1).</p><p><strong>What type of gene interaction is being shown?</strong></p>	These two genes show <strong>duplicate dominant epistasis</strong>. When either gene is dominant, it shows the same phenotype.	Incorrect	These two genes show <strong>duplicate interaction</strong>. When either gene is dominant, it hides the effects of the other gene.	Incorrect	These two genes show <strong>dominant and recessive epistasis</strong>. When one gene is dominant and another gene is homozygous recessive, it creates a new phenotype.	Incorrect	These two genes show <strong>digenic inheritance</strong>. Interaction of two genes affect the phenotypic expression of a single trait. The phenotypes were nine to seven (9:7).</p><p><strong>What type of gene interaction is being shown?</strong></p>	These two genes show <strong>duplicate dominant epistasis</strong>. When either gene is dominant, it shows the same phenotype.	Incorrect	These two genes show <strong>duplicate interaction</strong>. When either gene is dominant, it hides the effects of the other gene.	Incorrect	These two genes show <strong>recessive epistasis</strong>. When one gene is homozygous recessive, it hides the phenotype of the other gene.	Incorrect	These two genes show <strong>digenic inheritance</strong>. Interaction of two genes affect the phenotypic expression of a single trait.	Incorrect	These two genes show <strong>duplicate recessive epistasis</strong>. When either gene is homozygous recessive, it hides the effect of the other gene.	Correct	These two genes show <strong>dominant and recessive epistasis</strong>. When one gene is dominant and another gene is homozygous recessive, it creates a new phenotype.	Incorrect	These two genes show <strong>dominant epistasis</strong>. When one gene is dominant, it hides the phenotype of the other gene.	Incorrect

The phenotypes were fifteen to one (15:1).</p><p><strong>What type of gene interaction is being shown?</strong></p>	These two genes show <strong>duplicate interaction</strong>. When either gene is dominant, it hides the effects of the other gene.	Incorrect	These two genes show <strong>dominant epistasis</strong>. When one gene is dominant, it hides the phenotype of the other gene.	Incorrect	These two genes show <strong>duplicate dominant epistasis</strong>. When either gene is dominant, it shows the same phenotype.	Correct	These two genes show <strong>dominant and recessive epistasis</strong>. When one gene is dominant and another gene is homozygous recessive, it creates a new phenotype.	Incorrect	These two genes show <strong>duplicate recessive epistasis</strong>. When either gene is homozygous recessive, it hides the effect of the other gene.	Incorrect	These two genes show <strong>recessive epistasis</strong>. When one gene is homozygous recessive, it hides the phenotype of the other gene.	Incorrect	These two genes show <strong>digenic inheritance</strong>. Interaction of two genes affect the phenotypic expression of a single trait.	Incorrect
